                function t.ButtonEffect()
                    local O = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
                    local A = Drawing.new("Circle")
                    A.Visible = true
                    A.Radius = 10
                    A.Filled = true
                    A.Color = getgenv().UIColor["Click Effect Color"]
                    A.Position = Vector2.new(O.X, O.Y + 35)
                    local M = Instance.new("Folder")
                    M.Parent = Gui
                    M.Name = "Game nhu buoi"
                    local o = Instance.new("NumberValue")
                    o.Value = 10
                    o.Parent = M
                    o.Name = "Rua nhu buoi"
                    local W = Instance.new("NumberValue")
                    W.Value = 1
                    W.Parent = M
                    W.Name = "Rua nhu buoi 2"
                    J:Create(o, TweenInfo.new(.25), {Value = 25}):Play()
                    J:Create(W, TweenInfo.new(.25), {Value = 0}):Play()
                    o:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(
                        function()
                            A.Radius = o.Value
                        end
                    )
                    W:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(
                        function()
                            A.Transparency = W.Value
                        end
                    )
                    wait(.5)
                    M:Destroy()
                end
                t.GetIMG = function(O)
                    local A = "SynAsset ["
                    local M = ""
                    if string.find(O, "rbxassetid://") then
                        M = O
                    else
                        pcall(
                            function()
                                if O and type(O) == "string" and tostring(game:HttpGet(O)):find("PNG") then
                                    for o = 1, 5 do
                                        A = tostring(A .. string.char(math.random(65, 122)))
                                    end
                                    A = A .. "].png"
                                    writefile(A, game:HttpGet(O))
                                    spawn(
                                        function()
                                            wait(5)
                                            delfile(A)
                                        end
                                    )
                                    M = getsynasset(A)
                                end
                            end
                        )
                    end
                    return M
                end

                function Library.CreateMain(O)
                    local A = tostring(O.Title) or "Silver Hub"
                    getgenv().MainDesc = O.Desc or ""

                    cac = false
                    local function o(m7, c7)
                        local R7 = nil

                    local function ns()
                        for m7, c7 in pairs(us:GetChildren()) do
                            if not c7:IsA("UIListLayout") then
                                if string.find(string.lower(c7.Name), string.lower(gs.Text)) then
                                    c7.Visible = true
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    gs:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(
                        function()
                            zs()
                            ns()
                        end
                    )

                                local function Xq(iq)
                                    return {math.floor(iq.r * 255), math.floor(iq.g * 255), math.floor(iq.b * 255)}
                                end
                                local function Wq(iq)
                                    iq = iq:gsub("#", ""):upper():gsub("0X", "")
                                    return Color3.fromRGB(
                                        tonumber(iq:sub(1, 2), 16),
                                        tonumber(iq:sub(3, 4), 16),
                                        tonumber(iq:sub(5, 6), 16)
                                    )
                                end
                                local function Cq(iq)
                                    local Nq, Gq, Qq =
                                        string.format("%X", math.floor(iq.R * 255)),
                                        string.format("%X", math.floor(iq.G * 255)),
                                        string.format("%X", math.floor(iq.B * 255))
                                    if #Nq < 2 then
                                        Nq = "0" .. Nq
                                    end
                                    if #Gq < 2 then
                                        Gq = "0" .. Gq
                                    end
                                    if #Qq < 2 then
                                        Qq = "0" .. Qq
                                    end
                                    return string.format("%s%s%s", Nq, Gq, Qq)
                                end
                                p7, E7, l7 = 1, 1, 1

                                    if iq > Nq then
                                        return iq, Nq
                                    else

                                    end
                                end
                                local function wq(iq, Nq)
                                    if iq + Nq > 255 then
                                        local Gq, Qq = gq(iq, Nq)
                                        local Kq = 255 - Gq
                                        local vq, Uq = gq(Kq, Qq)
                                        return (vq - Uq)
                                    else
                                        return (iq + Nq)
                                    end
                                end
                                function CongColor(iq, Nq)
                                    local Gq, Qq = iq, Nq
                                    local Kq = math.sqrt
                                    local vq = {}
                                    vq.R = 255 - Kq(((255 - Gq.R) ^ 2 + (255 - Qq.R) ^ 2) / 2)
                                    vq.G = 255 - Kq(((255 - Gq.G) ^ 2 + (255 - Qq.G) ^ 2) / 2)
                                    vq.B = 255 - Kq(((255 - Gq.B) ^ 2 + (255 - Qq.B) ^ 2) / 2)
                                    return Color3.new(vq.R, vq.G, vq.B)
                                end

                    function GetGMT0()
                        local t = os.time()

                    function formatNumber(t)
                        return tostring(t):reverse():gsub("%d%d%d", "%1,"):reverse():gsub("^,", "")
                    end
                    function GetData(t)

                    function SplitStringByCapitalLetters(t)
                        return string.sub(string.gsub(t, "(%u)", " %1"), 2, -1.0)
                    end
                    function GetOwnFS()
                        local t = {}
                        for J, D in pairs(_) do
                            if CommF:InvokeServer(D, true) == 1 then

                    function GetBloxFruitChild(t)
                        for J, D in ipairs(t:GetChildren()) do
                            if D:IsA("Tool") and string.find(D.Name, "-") then
                                return D
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    function GetAwakenedMove(t)
                        if not t then
                            return
                        end
                        local J = t:FindFirstChild("AwakenedMoves")
                        if not J then
                            return
                        end
                        local D = {}
                        for p, s in ipairs(J:GetChildren()) do
                            D[s.Name] = true
                        end
                        return D
                    end
                    function WriteStats()
                        local t = GetOwnFS()
                        local J = {}
                        local D = {}
                        local p = {}
                        local s = {}
                        for M, o in pairs(
                            getupvalue(require(plr.PlayerGui.Main.UIController.Inventory).UpdateRender, 4)
                        ) do
                            for W, n in pairs(q) do
                                if o.details.Rarity == n then
                                    if not J[W] then
                                        J[W] = {}
                                    end
                                    if not D[W] then
                                        D[W] = {}
                                    end
                                    if not p[W] then
                                        p[W] = {}
                                    end
                                    if not s[W] then
                                        s[W] = {}
                                    end
                                    if o.details.Type == "Sword" then
                                        table.insert(J[W], o.details.Name)
                                    elseif o.details.Type == "Blox Fruit" then
                                        table.insert(D[W], o.details.Name)
                                    elseif o.details.Type == "Accessory" then
                                        table.insert(p[W], o.details.Name)
                                    elseif o.details.Type == "Material" then
                                        table.insert(s[W], o.details.Name)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        if IsHaveItem("Soul Guitar") then
                            k = "Mythical"
                            if not J[k] then
                                J[k] = {}
                            end
                            table.insert(J[k], "Soul Guitar")
                        end
                        for M, o in pairs(q) do
                            if not J[M] then
                                J[M] = {}
                            end
                            if not D[M] then
                                D[M] = {}
                            end
                            if not p[M] then
                                p[M] = {}
                            end
                            if not s[M] then
                                s[M] = {}
                            end
                        end
                        local O = GetBloxFruitChild(plr.Backpack) or GetBloxFruitChild(plr.Character)
                        local A = GetAwakenedMove(O)
                        if not A then
                            A = {}
                        end
                        if OutputData["Type"] == "string" or myAccount then
                            local M = ""
                            function AddData(h)
                                M = M .. h .. "\10"
                            end
                            AddData("- Level: " .. GetData("Level"))
                            AddData("- Fragments: " .. GetData("Fragments"))
                            AddData("- Beli: " .. GetData("Beli"))
                            AddData("- Race: " .. GetData("Race"))
                            AddData("- Blox Fruit: " .. GetData("DevilFruit") or "None")
                            AddData("- World: " .. x[0][1][x[0][2]][game.PlaceId])
                            local o = x[1][1][x[1][2]]()
                            AddData("- Script Status: ")
                            AddData(" + Auto Farm: " .. o["Auto Farm"])
                            AddData(" + Auto Item: " .. o["Auto Item"])
                            AddData("- Fighting Style: ")
                            local W
                            for h, bs in ipairs(GetOwnFS()) do
                                W = true
                                AddData(" + " .. bs)
                            end
                            if not W then
                                AddData(" + None")
                            end
                            AddData("- Sword Inventory: ")
                            local n
                            for h, bs in pairs(J) do
                                for Zs, xs in ipairs(bs) do
                                    n = true
                                    AddData(" + " .. "[" .. h .. "] " .. xs)
                                end
                            end
                            if not n then
                                AddData(" + None")
                            end
                            AddData("- Blox Fruit Inventory: ")
                            local e
                            for h, bs in pairs(D) do
                                for Zs, xs in ipairs(bs) do
                                    e = true
                                    AddData(" + " .. "[" .. h .. "] " .. xs)
                                end
                            end
                            if not e then
                                AddData(" + None")
                            end
                            AddData("- Accessory Inventory: ")
                            local L
                            for h, bs in pairs(p) do
                                for Zs, xs in ipairs(bs) do
                                    L = true
                                    AddData(" + " .. "[" .. h .. "] " .. xs)
                                end
                            end
                            if not L then
                                AddData(" + None")
                            end
                            AddData("- Material Inventory: ")
                            local f
                            for h, bs in pairs(s) do
                                for Zs, xs in ipairs(bs) do
                                    f = true
                                    AddData(" + " .. "[" .. h .. "] " .. xs)
                                end
                            end
                            if not f then
                                AddData(" + None")
                            end
                            AddData("- Awakened Move: ")
                            local K
                            for h, bs in pairs(A) do
                                K = true
                                AddData(" + " .. h)
                            end
                            if not K then
                                AddData(" + None")
                            end
                            if myAccount then
                                myAccount:SetDescription(M)
                            else
                                writefile(plr.Name .. ".datas", M)
                            end
                        elseif OutputData["Type"] == "json" then
                            local M =
                                game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONEncode(
                                {
                                    Level = GetData("Level"),
                                    Fragments = GetData("Fragments"),
                                    Beli = GetData("Beli"),
                                    Race = GetData("Race"),
                                    DevilFruit = GetData("DevilFruit"),
                                    World = x[0][1][x[0][2]][game.PlaceId],
                                    ScriptStatus = x[1][1][x[1][2]](),
                                    FightingStyle = t,
                                    Inventory = {
                                        Sword = {
                                            Common = J["Common"],
                                            Uncommon = J["Uncommon"],
                                            Rare = J["Rare"],
                                            Legendary = J["Legendary"],
                                            Mythical = J["Mythical"]
                                        },
                                        BloxFruit = {
                                            Common = D["Common"],
                                            Uncommon = D["Uncommon"],
                                            Rare = D["Rare"],
                                            Legendary = D["Legendary"],
                                            Mythical = D["Mythical"]
                                        },
                                        Accessory = {
                                            Common = p["Common"],
                                            Uncommon = p["Uncommon"],
                                            Rare = p["Rare"],
                                            Legendary = p["Legendary"],
                                            Mythical = p["Mythical"]
                                        },
                                        Material = {
                                            Common = s["Common"],
                                            Uncommon = s["Uncommon"],
                                            Rare = s["Rare"],
                                            Legendary = s["Legendary"],
                                            Mythical = s["Mythical"]
                                        }
                                    },
                                    AwakenedMove = {
                                        Z = A["Z"],
                                        X = A["X"],
                                        C = A["C"],
                                        V = A["V"],
                                        F = A["F"],
                                        TAP = A["TAP"]
                                    }
                                }
                            )
                            writefile(plr.Name .. ".datas", M)
                        end
                    end
                    if OutputData["Cooldown"] < 60 then
                        OutputData["Cooldown"] = 60
                    end
                    spawn(
                        function()
                            wait(1)
                            while wait() do
                                if OutputData["Type"] == "RAM" then
                                    local t =
                                        loadstring(
                                        game:HttpGet(
                                            "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ic3w0lf22/Roblox-Account-Manager/master/RAMAccount.lua"
                                        )
                                    )()
                                    getgenv().myAccount = t.new(plr.Name)
                                    if not myAccount then
                                        warn("Account not found on Roblox Account Manager")
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                                pcall(
                                    function()
                                        if not GetDataDelay or tick() - GetDataDelay >= OutputData["Cooldown"] then
                                            getgenv().GetDataDelay = tick()
                                            WriteStats()
                                        end
                                    end
                                )
                                wait(5)
                            end
                        end
                    )
                end
            end
        end
    },
    {0XE02B, 4255488762, 377365500, 4183726611, 3202403033, 3346673392, 0X2C29F2B2, 3542870230, 3133529520}
)(...);
